  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1d72466b-aece-4848-91dc-3cb530126827'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer17461640004703519202">This book is all about Meghan's little brother, Ethan. Of course, Ethan is a teenager now and he's really cool. =) <br/><br/>I loved that he took Kali in the book because I used to take that before I got sick! I loved it so much and I love that the author added it into the book =) <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494006608i/22675479._SX540_.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494006608i/22675480.jpg' alt=' : ' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ethan can see the Fey, he always could since he was a young boy.   <span id="freeText17461640004703519202" style="display:none">This book is all about Meghan's little brother, Ethan. Of course, Ethan is a teenager now and he's really cool. =) <br><br>I loved that he took Kali in the book because I used to take that before I got sick! I loved it so much and I love that the author added it into the book =) <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494006608i/22675479._SX540_.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494006608i/22675480.jpg" alt=" : " class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ethan can see the Fey, he always could since he was a young boy. He tries his best to ignore them so they won't catch on, but it doesn't work out too good. <br><br>He has changed schools several times because of what people think is bad behavior. In reality it's Ethan fighting off the fey or running from them. <br><br>In his new school, Ethan ends up becoming friends with Todd, who is a half fey. Ethan doesn't want to be friends with anyone but it happens. He also takes up with Kenzie who is on the school newspaper and is relentless in getting a story out of him. We all know she ends up a love interest, right? <br><br>At one point Todd goes missing and the Ethan has to search for him. Of course, Kenzie brings herself along. It turns out there are these bad fey out there kidnapping half-fey. What are they doing to them? I'm not telling you, but it's narly. <br><br>Ethan ends up back in Nevernever when he calls in his favor to his sister, Meghan, the Iron Queen. We do get to have some cameo's from Grim, Meghan, Ash and Puck. I miss them all! <br><br>Keirran who is Ethan's nephew decides he's going to help them out. He's part fey as well and he lives in Nevernever. <br><br>They end up going on a little cray adventure with the help of Leanansidhe, she's in it again too and she makes it to where Kenzie can see the fey. Kenzie is just human and can't see them but now she can. <br><br>Anyway, I thought it was good and I hope the next two books are good as well! =)<br><br>MY BLOG: <a href="http://melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com/2017/05/the-lost-prince-by-julie-kagawa.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Melissa Martin's Reading List</a></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText8515056519869862148" style="display:none">The Lost Prince (The Iron Fey: Call of the Forgotten #1), Julie Kagawa<br /><br />The Lost Prince follows the character of Eleanor Burden, an 1890's Boston socialite who has resigned herself to marrying the man she should be with rather than the man she wants, whom she lost in Vienna. <br /><br />What separates her from others of her station and background is that Eleanor believes that she has the ability to predict all of the major historical events that will occur while she is alive. <br /><br />Dismissed as a hysteric, Eleanor must decide whether or not fate is predetermined or if she possesses the ability to change future events as well as her own life.<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش روز هجدهم ماه فوریه سال 2020 میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: شاهزاده گم‌شده؛ نویسنده: جولی کاگاوا؛ مترجم: نجلا محقق؛ دبیر مجموعه نیما کهندانی؛ تهران: نشر باژ‏‫، 1398؛ در 348ص؛ فروست مجموعه رویازاد آهنین؛ شابک 9786222192280؛ موضوع: داستانهای نویسندگان ایالات متحده آمریکا - سده 21م<br /><br />آیا او توانایی تغییر رویدادهای آینده و همچنین زندگی خودش و رویاها را دارد؛ <br /><br />تاریخ بهنگام رسانی 27/03/1399هجری خورشیدی؛ ا. شربیانی</span>

<div id="review_255282837" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/255282837" />
    <a title="Soumi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6833452-soumi"><img alt="Soumi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440767658p2/6833452.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6833452-soumi?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer255282837" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5871318658217481335"><b>“I can’t stop it. I can’t stop Them from following me. If it was just me that the fey picked on, I’d be okay with that. But someone else always pays for my Sight. Someone else always gets hurt instead of me.” Tearing my gaze from hers, I looked out over the fields. “I’d rather be alone,” I muttered, “then to have to watch that again.”</b><br/><br/>Do you remember the little boy who was kidnapped by a vicious fey, and his big sister set out a journey to find that kind to a strange and magical place called Neve</span>
  <span id="freeText5871318658217481335" style="display:none"><b>“I can’t stop it. I can’t stop Them from following me. If it was just me that the fey picked on, I’d be okay with that. But someone else always pays for my Sight. Someone else always gets hurt instead of me.” Tearing my gaze from hers, I looked out over the fields. “I’d rather be alone,” I muttered, “then to have to watch that again.”</b><br><br>Do you remember the little boy who was kidnapped by a vicious fey, and his big sister set out a journey to find that kind to a strange and magical place called NeverNever. Well, guess what, after a time leap of twelve years, that little boy has grown into a handsome hunk. Yes, that boy is Ethan Chase and he is back with a bang. <br><br>The Iron Fey is my all-time favorite YA novel series. When I mourning over why the series came to an end, then Julie Kagawa announced there is going to be a spin off and my heart stared hammering against my ribs. And when I finally managed to get my claws on a pretty ARC and I finished the story, nausea gripped my mind in excitement and I took an entire week to collect words and wrap my thoughts around it. <br><br><b>A Prince on A Mission</b><br><br>Ethan always wanted to stay from anything relates to the magical fey realm or fairies. The nightmarish memories from his childhood of being a prisoner in enormous iron castle is still haunting his so badly that his heart is nothing but full of hatred against entire fey kind. He even blames them for the distance that has formed between him and his older sister Megan, who fell in love with one of them and left their family. Hence Ethan wouldn't dare to think or look at the fey kind; neither could he let them know about his existence or his power to see through the glamour of fairies. Hence when his half breed friend got kidnapped by a new and vicious race of forgotten fairies, and they stared chasing Ethan too, he was forced to enter in the world of NeverNever he despair most, and along with the girl he would never dare to fall for. Of on his mission we see a not so happy family reunion; we again met the icy prince and the great prankster, the dark muse and our beloved fur-ball. <br><br><b>Ethan, Kenzie and Keirran</b><br><br>Ethan was kind of brooding and smoking hot, also occasional jerk-ass. I could help but mentioning how Ethan somehow reminded me of Ash. Ethan has always kept a bad boy image to build a barrier around hi true self, kind of the icy walls Ash used to shield his soft interior. But as the book progressed, we saw who Ethan Chase is actually deep down. The façade of rudeness and a tough guy image is just a cover for his rebellious spirit, his true feelings for the girl he is afraid to fall in love with and the pain and the anger he is carrying with him. <br>He has no fey magic to fight of the evils; he is just a human teenage boy who is extraordinarily skilled in martial arts. When I first read about Ethan, he was a toddler, now it’s strange to read about him that he has grown into a hot-ass hero. <br><br>However I’m more impressed by the female protagonist Mackenzie St. James or Kenzie, as we call her. She was just kick-ass as any boys of her age, and also the girl who secretly melted Ethan’s heart. She much more than what is seems to be, I just can’t stop appalling for her. She made me smile, and brought tears in my eyes as the same time. She didn’t flinch to make deals with fairies; she didn’t back away from Ethan, even if she was gravely unwell to go on with him. She was fearless of any incoming danger, audacious explorer who wants to see everything and experience them. You rock girl.<br><br>Now talking about Keirran, I just don’t believe Ash is his father, I mean what the freaking hell, Ash became a father? Really?<br>However half-fey and half human Keirran was shadow of Meghan, rather than Ash, and he got same features as her, and skills as Ash, swift and deadly. Keirran is master extraordinary power; he can exert three kinds of magic, summer, winter and Iron. He played a major role in The Lost Prince, he accompanied Ethan and Kenzie into their quest <i>(imagine Ethan has a nephew of same age)</i> and fought battles beside them. I wonder why Puck mentioned Ethan and Keirran reminded him about a certain pair <i>(Rings a bell? Yeah, he was talking about him and Ash, and their golden old days)</i><br><br><b>The Old Legends</b><br><br>Well, when we are talking about the spin off of The iron Fey, how can we possibly forget to mention our Iron Legends, Meghan, Ash, Puck <i>(ohhh Baby!!!)</i> and Grimalkin. Meghan is no longer that teenager girl we knew; she is now ruler of Iron realm, more powerful and responsible. Still handsome as ever, Ash is Meghan’s iron Knight, and father of her son (sigh!). <br>Well, good news is my Puck, the prankster is single <i>(and ready to be mingled with me)</i>. He appeared only twice in the book, and both time he kicked some ass <i>(Yo love, you rock)</i>. <br>My cutie Grimalkin was with the trio for all the time, and who could be the best guide to NeverNever other than him. <br><br><b>Overall Thoughts</b> <br><br>As a fan of The Iron Fey series, I had very high expectation for The Lost Prince, and I was breathlessly waiting for the book to come out quickly. And, I was again spellbound by my favorite storyteller, author Julie Kagawa. Her gorgeous prose and amazing story weaving kept me hooked on the book until late night. Any Iron Fey fan in any corner of the world wouldn't dare to miss the book, and I bet my money on that.<br><br><br><b>Update 15-10-2012 :</b> just finished with The Lost prince, and fainted each time Puck appeared. Also, Kenzie, you girl rocks and you made me cry. I so want to be you best friend now .<br><br><b>Update 17/08/2012</b> I just got my copy, not a digital one, a 100% read print ARC. My god. It looks so yummy. *faints* <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380250664ra/681981.gif" width="386" height="258" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380366291ra/718482.gif" width="320" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Goodness, .. Ethan is so damn fucking hot, I need oxygen and the first chapter behind The Immortal Rules ARC made me hungry for this book so so so much <br>Holy freak, Hell yeah</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366291i/718483.jpg" width="200" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5871318658217481335" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/408335642?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=to-ya-or-not-to-ya">to-ya-or-not-to-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=fun-fantasy">fun-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=ya-pnr-maddness">ya-pnr-maddness</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer408335642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16813699459213181953">Look, last time I knew Ethan he was a five years old. Please tell me I'm not the only one conflicted about the boy on the cover! I almost didn't want to read this book because I kept expecting Chris Hansen to come in and tell me to take a seat.<br/><br/>Then I'd be like, "I swear! He's sixteen! I just READ about him when he was five! He's totally of age now!"<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390272i/751882._SX540_.jpg' alt='crying girl' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Then I'd cry dramatically JUST like this.</i><br/><br/>But, facts are facts, folks. Ethan's aged like a fine brandy if brandy had washboard abs and a butt built fo</span>
  <span id="freeText16813699459213181953" style="display:none">Look, last time I knew Ethan he was a five years old. Please tell me I'm not the only one conflicted about the boy on the cover! I almost didn't want to read this book because I kept expecting Chris Hansen to come in and tell me to take a seat.<br><br>Then I'd be like, "I swear! He's sixteen! I just READ about him when he was five! He's totally of age now!"<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390272i/751882._SX540_.jpg" alt="crying girl" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Then I'd cry dramatically JUST like this.</i><br><br>But, facts are facts, folks. Ethan's aged like a fine brandy if brandy had washboard abs and a butt built for spanking. AAAAAAaaaaaannndd, I just reach my creepy quota for the review. Wow. That didn't take long.<br><br>So Ethan meets up with Love-Interest while trying to avoid the Fae working their darndest to ruin his life. To save his and the Love-Interest's life they escape into Fairyland to track down his sister and solve the mystery and try to save the world.<br><br>More Facts: you don't need to have read the Iron Fey series to read this book. There's enough back history and explanatory exposition to make it through. I certainly haven't read The Iron Fey series and I managed to enjoy this one as a standalone.<br><br>Like angst? Ethan's your main dude. Seriously. Kid could bottle that stuff. I'm sure there's a roaring trade in teenage self-pity tears. But he's balanced out so nicely with Kenzie who would, by herself, be kind of a meh character. I might have found them both insufferably frustrating except they seemed to bring out the best in each other. So if teenage hot boy angst is your thing - hit this one up! It has it in spades.<br><br>Other than that you have all your old friends back. Meghan, Ash, Grimalkin, Puck et all and then you have some newer ones and then you have a pretty decent and solid mystery/action story going on.<br><br>Julie Kagawa's come along way since the first novel of hers that I read, The Iron King. I didn't get bored, kept eye rolling to a minimum and largely enjoyed the narrative.<br><br>There's one young man in the book though, I won't mention who he is. But I will say this: Son. SON! Don't go breaking our hearts, m'kay? You've reduced me to quoting Elton John here. It doesn't get more serious than this.<br><br> <br><br>So, over all summation is that I want to hunt down the Iron Fey series and read that. Then I want to hunt down the novellas and read them. Then I want to start badgering the Harlequin Teen's publicist to put me on the list for the next one. I'd say that's a ringing endorsement. Wouldn't you?</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rimsha Salam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rimsha Salam" href="/user/show/6090854-rimsha-salam">Rimsha Salam</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6090854-rimsha-salam?shelf=made-me-scream">made-me-scream</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6090854-rimsha-salam?shelf=swoon-worthy">swoon-worthy</a>,

<div id="review_208418716" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/208418716" />
    <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair"><img alt="Steph Sinclair" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1457555690p2/4642710.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/208418716?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph Sinclair" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair">Steph Sinclair</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Iron Fey fans </span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=fey">fey</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2-am-or-later">2-am-or-later</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=e-arc">e-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2012-favs">2012-favs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=i-need-the-next-book-like-yesterday">i-need-the-next-book-like-yesterday</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=best-characters">best-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer208418716" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12559945011658536342"><br/>Actual rating: 4.5 stars. <br/><br/>Show of hands. How many of you were worried about Kagawa returning to the Nevernever with a spin-off of an already successful series? *raises hand* I mean, let's think about this for a minute. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9659607-the-iron-knight' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <em>The Iron Knight</em>
</a> concluded and it seemed everything was "happy happy, joy joy," right? But then there were whisperings in the wind of a spin-off and I found myself saying, "What?! NOOO! NO, Julie! I forbid it! Ya hear?!" At the time the saying "Don't beat a dead horse" was runn</span>
  <span id="freeText12559945011658536342" style="display:none"><br>Actual rating: 4.5 stars. <br><br>Show of hands. How many of you were worried about Kagawa returning to the Nevernever with a spin-off of an already successful series? *raises hand* I mean, let's think about this for a minute. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9659607-the-iron-knight" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <em>The Iron Knight</em>
</a> concluded and it seemed everything was "happy happy, joy joy," right? But then there were whisperings in the wind of a spin-off and I found myself saying, "What?! NOOO! NO, Julie! I forbid it! Ya hear?!" At the time the saying "Don't beat a dead horse" was running through my head and I was so nervous about this new endeavor. If I'm being honest here, spin-offs usually suck big time. But just like in the case of <em><a title="ARC Book Review: Immortal Rules by Julie Kagawa" href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/2012/04/arc-book-review-immortal-rules-by-julie-kagawa/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a>,</em> Julie Kagawa has put me in my place saying, "I got this, YO." And boy, did she ever! <em>The Lost Prince</em> is everything I could want and more. With fresh new characters, cameo appearances and a new evil threatening the Nevernever, how could anyone resist?<br><br>Before I begin, I need to get something out of my system.<br><br>PUCK!! I LOVE YOU!<br><br>*clears throat*<br><br>What? Don't judge me!<br><br>Remember the little boy from <em><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6644117-the-iron-king" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Iron King</a>?</em> Meghan's little brother? Did you ever wonder what happened to him and his family once Meghan had gone off for good with her Ice Prince to rule in the Nevernever as a Queen of Faery? That's just what <em>The Lost Prince</em> does. And let me tell you, Ethan Chase is not what I expected. The years of being tormented by the fey and losing his sister to their world has made him a very bitter and angry person. Honestly, I don't blame the guy. He has to constantly look over his shoulder, attempt to pretend They don't exist so as not to draw attention to himself, push people away so they don't catch the eyes of The Good Neighbors. It's a lot of responsibilities for anyone, let alone a teen boy (and yes, he actually <em>sounds</em> like a teen boy). But this is what he has had to endure all his life hopping from school to school due to "bad behavior." Unfortunately for Ethan, the fey just can't seem to stay away from him and he ends up on a quest to save the Nevernever.<br><br>The plot was brilliantly done. The characters were brilliant. This book was &gt;insert any positive adjective here<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9659607-the-iron-knight" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Iron Knight</a> correctly. But even as someone who has followed this series very closely, I have to admit, I have no idea what direction it could possibly go.<br><br>The one thing I was worried about most with this spin-off would be comparing the old characters to the new characters. I LOVED the trio in the original series. Meghan, Ash and Puck were the perfect blend of romantic tension, banter and comic relief. And they all <em>do</em> make cameo appearances (Did I mention how much I love Puck?), but this isn't their story. It's Ethan, Kenzie and Kierran's. I really think fans will really enjoy the new trio and it seems like Kagawa has us in for a world of hurt with them too. I mean, I bawled by eyes out so hard with <em><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8685612-the-iron-queen" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Iron Queen</a>. </em>Whenever I go back to read that last scene I fall to pieces.  But it feels like <em>that</em> could come a lot sooner with <em>The Call of the Forgotten.</em> MY EMOTIONS! Kagawa, stop being so awesome all. the. time! Wait...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380358916i/710079.png" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><em>#DontStop</em><br><br>And you know what? Even if you haven't read <em>The Iron Fey</em> - which you'd better go do if you haven't *gives dagger eyes* - you could still follow along easily to this story. For those who have been waiting for a certain Cait Sith (no relation to the cat pictured above, of course) to guide you back through the Nevernever, this will merely feel like a continuation from the original series. And you noobs? There are a few rules you must familiarize yourself with: <em>Never</em> make a contract with Them. Show no fear when dealing with the Fair Folk. Don't draw attention to yourself. And as Grim would say, "Do try and keep up." Welcome to Faery.<br><br><em>ARC was provided by the publisher via NetGalley. Thank you!</em><br><br>Want to win an ARC of The Lost Prince? Head on over to <a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Cuddlebuggery Book Blog</a> for a giveaway and other fantastical things.<br><br>----------------<br><br>OMG, guys! This is on NetGalley!! <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://netgalley.com/PopupHandler.php?module=catalog&amp;func=galleyTitleDetails&amp;projectid=19138">http://netgalley.com/PopupHandler.php...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12559945011658536342" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer229257542" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1057524643396617677">I have just finished reading Ash and Meghan's story and fell deeply in love with these characters, all of them! The Iron Knight had me in tears, especially the last paragraph, I don't know if it was because it was goodbye, knowing I won't be captured anymore by these characters and their quests, but it left me with a hole in my heart, a void that needs to be filled, but when I saw she was coming out with a spin off my heart beat a million times faster! can not wait for this series to come out!<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>He</span>
  <span id="freeText1057524643396617677" style="display:none">I have just finished reading Ash and Meghan's story and fell deeply in love with these characters, all of them! The Iron Knight had me in tears, especially the last paragraph, I don't know if it was because it was goodbye, knowing I won't be captured anymore by these characters and their quests, but it left me with a hole in my heart, a void that needs to be filled, but when I saw she was coming out with a spin off my heart beat a million times faster! can not wait for this series to come out!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Hello all, I have finally read this and it did not disappoint at all!<br /> I loved hear from Ethan, though his story was sad, dark and very depressing, but hey I guess that's the other half. The story after someone is taken, how their lives change so dramatically and how they have to pick up the pieces. Now keep a very open mind, this is nothing like the other books, this is Ethan's story, you will see some very familiar characters here and there, but this book offers new ones in the place of old. I was happy to see those oh so familiar names jump out in my page, but I felt there place was in the shadows, where it should be, and hopefully they will remain. I don't mind if they make guest appearances here and there, but I want the focus to be mainly on these new ones. The last books gave me the feeling of being pulled into som place magical and wonderful! Where as this book, I see it for what it is to be a human, scary, uninviting and real! Julie kagawa did a wonderful job and I can't wait for this new series to take shape</span>

<div id="review_231330885" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/231330885" />
    <a title="Maria " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5769334-maria"><img alt="Maria " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600318539p2/5769334.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/231330885?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria " href="/user/show/5769334-maria">Maria </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer231330885" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14549713499421010091"><b>MY REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK</b><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/thumbs%20up%20gif/Soumaya_Mouak/GIF-3.gif?o=1' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/excited%20gif/B_Bella/Gifs/excited.gif?o=14' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/274810.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirling%20gifs/MeggsieOnline/gifs/tumblr_lwdgnk90bg1r44blo.gif?o=24' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br/><br/>Yep! I have fallen crazy in love with this book. I mean I already know Julie Kagawa has a wicked imagination and writing skills but this book exceeded my expectations. Although the The Iron Fey: Call of the Forgotten share the same world as the Iron Fey series this has an entirely new flavor and excitement to it. <br/><br/>Want to know why? <br/><br/>Read on!<br/><br/><b>THE GIST</b><br/><br/>Ethan Chase always had the Sight. Even as a little kid he always had the abilit</span>
  <span id="freeText14549713499421010091" style="display:none"><b>MY REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK</b><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/thumbs%20up%20gif/Soumaya_Mouak/GIF-3.gif?o=1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/excited%20gif/B_Bella/Gifs/excited.gif?o=14" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/274810.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/fangirling%20gifs/MeggsieOnline/gifs/tumblr_lwdgnk90bg1r44blo.gif?o=24" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>Yep! I have fallen crazy in love with this book. I mean I already know Julie Kagawa has a wicked imagination and writing skills but this book exceeded my expectations. Although the The Iron Fey: Call of the Forgotten share the same world as the Iron Fey series this has an entirely new flavor and excitement to it. <br><br>Want to know why? <br><br>Read on!<br><br><b>THE GIST</b><br><br>Ethan Chase always had the Sight. Even as a little kid he always had the ability to see the invisible world of the Fey. <br><br>Ethan had an unpleasant experience with the Fey when he was younger and not only that but he also lost someone important to him, his half-sister Meghan. For more info regarding this story, you guys should read the Iron Fey series starting with the Iron King. <br><br>As Ethan grew up, he learned that the while he has the Sight he could never be close to anyone. It made him elusive and distant. He thought that he was better off alone. He didn't want to let anybody in because he was afraid that when he did they'll only get hurt like what happened to a friend of his, Sam. He's never been the same since.<br><br>Starting over at a new school, he had planned everything. Just try to blend in, don't talk to anyone. But it seems that destiny has different plans for Ethan because the more he turns away from the Fey, the more they run after him.<br><br>Something was brewing. Something was out there. And Ethan was gonna find out what it is.<br><br><b>FIRST IMPRESSION</b><br><br>To tell you honestly, I already knew this book was gonna be awesome even before I read the summary from GR. I already knew that I was going to love it like the other books of Julie Kagawa. <br><br>And I was so right!<br><br>I got a extremely sad when the Iron Fey series ended. The world that Ms. Kagawa made on that series was surreal and enthralling and I was really hoping for more. It seems that she heard my prayers. <br><br>When I heard about the spin-off, i was enthusiastic that it was going to be another great series. When I read the summary, I was delirious with joy because it sounds awesome already. When I saw the cover, I was fervent. I needed that book!<br><br>I would like to thank NetGalley and Harlequin Teen for allowing me to review this book. It is an honor.<br><br><b>CHARACTERS</b><br><br><b>Ethan Chase</b><br><br>Ethan Chase, I didn't expect you to grow up to be this rebelious! You are so kick-ass! I couldn't believe it! You were so different from the kid I loved from the Iron Fey series. You are all grown up now and so... effin HOT!<br><br>I had a bit of an issue with Ethan at first being rude and distant and all the emo stuff. It was in my nerves a bit but then when you read more about what he had went through growing up you'll understand why he has been like that. <br><br>I love reading Ethan's POV as much as I did Meghan's. But this time it was more masculine and more darker than Meghan's.<br><br>Ethan did remind me of a certain Final Fantasy character who I also love but will reveal later.<br><br>PS: Reading about Ethan now makes me feel like I'm old enough to be his aunt or something. Hahaha. This is crazy! I can't seem to forget that the first time I read him he was so young and now he's all grown up now and so freakin' rebellious, it brings tears to my eyes. Tears of joy to be exact. It felt like I raised a kid! Hahah. What the heck?!<br><br><b>Mackenzie St. James</b><br><br>Oh I got to hand it to this girl, she is awesome. I just love her. I liked everything about her.<br><br>There is a lot going on with this girl than meets the eye. She was more than just the dauntless girl who wants to get Ethan's interview. She was more than just the girl who was willing to stay with Ethan despite everything. She wasn't whiny which I totally adored. She wasn't one who makes stupid decisions based on impulse, all her decisions meant something. What that decision is you'll just have to read through the book to find out. :)<br><br>What I learned about her near the end of the book was just a surprise. I loved her even more after that.<br><br><b>Prince Keirran</b><br><br>What can I say? I love Keirran because he was the son of the forever love of my life Ash. I have to love him! Just kidding!<br><br>He was half-fey, half-human but according to him he was 3/4 human. Which means she takes more from her mother but I very much doubt that. He was an equal of both Ash and Meghan. <br><br>Keirran along with Ethan would play a big role on the new developments that has being going around in NeverNever. There was something people around them aren't telling them and they knew it. <br><br>Keirran has powers that no one else had. He could weild Summer, Winter and Iron's magic. He was really something. But as they always say, "Great power comes great responsibility". I really wish he won't make some stupid decision because like his father he would do anything for love. I hope he doesn't in loads of trouble because of that.<br><br><b>Grimalkin</b><br><br>As usual, this cat still as apathetic as ever. I still loved him though. I missed reading about this vanishing cat! <br><br><b>Meghan, Ash and Puck</b><br><br>I missed these guys. They're still the same guys I've come to love from the original series although a bit more mature at that. I hope we get to see more of them here though. I like Ash being a dad. Seriously, cute. I wouldn't mind him fathering my kid! :)<br><br><b>ETHAN + KENZIE = CUTE SWEET LOVE</b><br><br>Ethan and Kenzie's relationship very much reminded me of Final Fantasy's Squall and Rinoa.<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/squall%20and%20rinoa/Stella31/Rinoa-x-Squall.gif?o=266" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713614.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/squall%20and%20rinoa/punkgika/FFVIII/Rinoa%20and%20Squall/00047.jpg?o=275" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380362518i/713615.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/squall%20and%20rinoa/SephirothForPresident/squall-rinoa-kiss-o.gif?o=288" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713616.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Seriously! <br><br>Ethan was like Squall because he was all passive and distant while Kenzie was all bubbly and positive. Kenzie touched Ethan in a way that Rinoa touched Squall. <br><br>There is a lot of similarities between them but I am not complaining. I loved Final Fantasy 8. Too bad they didn't make a movie out of it because that would have been great!<br><br>Ethan and Kenzie's relationship wasn't insta-love! *thank goodness!* It gradually unfolded. At first Ethan, may have thought Kenzie was pretty but he didn't feel attracted to her that much until she got to know her better, likewise with Kenzie. <br><br><b>KEIRRAN + ANNYWL = FORBIDDEN LOVE PART 2</b><br><br>We all know that Ash and Meghan were from different courts right? And being involved from someone from a different court was forbidden. Well their son sort of fallen in love with someone forbidden too.<br><br>Annywl was a Summer Fey who got exiled by Queen Titania because of some stupid reason. Keirran well fell in love. We all know how his father fell in love, this boy Keirran takes that from his father.<br><br>I just wish there something good is going to happen to these two.<br><br><b>HIGHLIGHTS</b><br><br>- Ethan's way of fighting was not like Keirran's. He uses a Filipino Martial Arts technique called Kali that I didn't know existed until now. I am a Filipino and I didn't know the use of Arnis (rattan sticks) was called Kali. This was seriously awesome!<br><br>- Ethan was also a highlight. He was a great but slightly annoying character.<br><br>- The antagonist for this series was definitely unexpected. I was kind of worried if they were gonna make the Iron Fey bad again but good thing Ms. Kagawa thought of something new and sinister.<br><br>- The plot development was awesome. It wasn't too fast, it wasn't too slow. It allows you take in all the details and enjoy the new ones as well.<br><br>- The fact that there was no lovetriangle was a big highlight for me. The love triangle in YA books is getting old for me. Good thing that Keirran has his own love story to tell. I mean from what I see on this book. I am not sure what Ms. Kagawa has up her sleeve but I am sure its good no matter what.<br><br>- NeverNever was still as spellbinding as ever. <br><br>- It was a balance of action and the now and then talks about what is happening around NeverNever.<br><br>- I liked that it didn't focus much about the romance aspect. I just wish it stays that way. <br><br>- Character development was awesome. Ethan developed gradually which I think was only right because you don't get a change of heart so quickly. Kenzie, on the other hand, was just so perfect for me. The unvealing of the secret was just a surprise for me. With Keirran, I am not really sure. There was something about his character that is still hidden and I want to find out about it now! :p <br><br>- The cover was just gorgeous. (don't you agree?)<br><br>- The ending was good. I don't like it when books end in a very abrupt cliffhanger. This book didn't. It ended in a way that there is closure for the intial book but still gives way to questions as to how the next book will start and end. <br><br><b>FINAL WORDS</b><br><br>This book is no Iron Fey series but for me it entirely lived up to my expectation and more. There was no place for disappointments for me as I was reading this book. I was just as enthralled as I was when I first read the Iron King. I wouldn't say that this book was better because its not. I'm not saying that its inferior because its not either. Let's just say that they both have a league of their own and I am totally in love with them both.<br><br>When I heard of the spin-off I knew that it was going to be amazing and after I read the book I knew I was right. Julie Kagawa was a story teller. It even made me think that maybe Julie has the Sight and she could see them just like Shakespeare that's why she was able to create the very vivid world of NeverNever and its inbelievably real characters. <br><br>I have to say though that no matter what happens, Ash would still be the only Fey in my heart. I mean I love Ethan and Keirran but I feel like an cougar falling for these two kids. (seriously, that was how it made me feel. like I'm an old woman crushing on these youngs kids. they could send me to jail for being a pedophile. hahaha) But yeah, I like them and everything but still it will always be Prince Ash for me.<br><br>This book filled the void in my heart when I read the last book of the Iron Fey series. I seriously thought I wouldn't be reading anything about the Feys that I come to love but Julie caught me off guard with another one of her masterpiece.<br><br>I want more. I am already addicted. I need more of this. It is like a drug to me already. I can't wait for the second book. I want to know who the Traitor Son is. But I think we already have a clue on who it is.<br><br><b>RATING: </b><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/star%20gif/kammy_189/star.gif?o=8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/star%20gif/kammy_189/star.gif?o=8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/star%20gif/kammy_189/star.gif?o=8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/star%20gif/kammy_189/star.gif?o=8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/star%20gif/kammy_189/star.gif?o=8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380362518ra/713617.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer400995065" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer764941902474899953"><b>Final rating: 4.5/5 stars</b><br/><b>Final rating - for the whole series: 4~4.25/5 stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389114i/750105._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>First things first. THIS BOOK WAS THE BEST IRON FEY BOOK EVER (well, depends xD it rivals with the Iron Queen)!!!!!</b> Why is that? Because I couldn’t stop reading, I loved all of the characters, the story and most of all – <b>there was no love triangle – VICTORY!!!</b><br/><br/><b>And look at this beautiful cover ♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1352034682l/16090769.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>I have one thing to say to the future readers: </b> if you have read <b>Iron’s prophecy </b>then you have <b>probably spoiled yourself</b> in a way </span>
  <span id="freeText764941902474899953" style="display:none"><b>Final rating: 4.5/5 stars</b><br><b>Final rating - for the whole series: 4~4.25/5 stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389114i/750105._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>First things first. THIS BOOK WAS THE BEST IRON FEY BOOK EVER (well, depends xD it rivals with the Iron Queen)!!!!!</b> Why is that? Because I couldn’t stop reading, I loved all of the characters, the story and most of all – <b>there was no love triangle – VICTORY!!!</b><br><br><b>And look at this beautiful cover ♥</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1352034682l/16090769.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I have one thing to say to the future readers: </b> if you have read <b>Iron’s prophecy </b>then you have <b>probably spoiled yourself</b> in a way for this book. If not, I suggest you read it after you read Lost prince. It will clear some things and it will be make you scream for the next one (not guaranteed, but high probability).<br><br><b>Also, this series can be read as standalone, for everything is explained, but you probably should read Iron Fey series first.</b><br><br><b>I was so happy to read about the old characters like Meghan, Puck, Grimalkin, Ash…..and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Leanansidhe <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but I loved the new set of characters as well!</b><br><br>P.s. those who plan to watch the TV show Firefly may be utterly and completely destroyed by spoilers xD<br><br><blockquote> <b>► STORY</b>: </blockquote><br><br><b><br>Short description of what happened in the Iron Fey world, but be warned, SPOILERs for those who haven't read it :D </b><br><br><i><br>There is an unknown world to the mortal race called <b>Nevernever,</b> home to all Fey. There were two courts once – <b>the Winter court,</b> ruled by Queen Mab, and <b>Summer court</b>, ruled by Lord Oberon and Queen Titania. But, when the new kingdom and race showed up, the fey of Iron and Technology – it led to war. (<i>continues in the spoiler</i>)<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The war stopped when the Iron Queen, Meghan Chase, a half breed daughter of Oberon took the throne of the Iron Kingdom. Many years have passed in the human world since Meghan Chase became the Iron Queen. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This time, <b>the story follows</b> Meghan's (heroine from the Iron Fey series) stepbrother<b> Ethan who has the gift of the Sight </b>since he was born.<br><br> Life wasn’t easy for Ethan – <b>having the sight goes both ways: he can see them, but they notice him too. </b>And when they do, they torment that person for the rest of his/her life. Being able to see them made him seem like a troublemaker in the eyes of other people, which often lead to him being expelled from schools or having to go to another. <br><br>When he transfers in the new school, on the first day he meets Kenzie, a reporter who is quite interested in him. But he also saved half breed Todd who got into trouble with bullies. But when Todd accidentally finds out that Ethan is able to see them, he asks for help. Something dark is lurking in the shadows around his home and he needs protection. But Ethan, being distrustful of all fey, helps him because he thought that Todd won’t bother him anymore. But when Todd mysteriously disappears and when a creepy fey attacks Ethan in front of Kenzie, they are forced to flee into the Nevernever, to seek help from the Iron Queen.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Those who have read the Iron Knight, can remember the fey called the Forgotten.</b> Well, it is pretty much obvious which Fey we are reading about this time. Anyway, i think they were nice (and scary) addition to the series and i enjoyed it. I cannot wait to see what will happen in the next books ( and i am beginning to dread the outcome of it)<br><br><br><blockquote> <b>► CHARACTERS</b>: </blockquote><br><br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Ethan </u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br><b>Ethan has hated the Fey his whole life. </b>After the trauma he suffered as a four year old kid, he learned that the fey are never to be trusted, bargained with or thanked. <br><br>He found out as much as he could about them so he could defend himself, even practicing Kali, a Filipino martial art, which taught defense with sticks, knives and swords. <br><br>He never lets anyone get close to him, because of fear that fey may hurt them; he acts as a <b>“Bad Boy”</b>. This earned him a serious troublemaker reputation. So when he transfers to new school, one persistent girl, Kenzie, wants to interview him. He couldn’t even begin to imagine how persistent she would turn out to be.<br><br><b> Ethan is one of the characters I actually liked</b> (even when he was acting like douchebag xD). He may be jackass sometimes, but I understood him, it was not his fault - BUT, be warned, he is quite angsty - woe is me type of character, brooding and so on...(<i>that seriously irritated me sometimes, but i dont blame him</i>).<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “Well, well,” answered a cool, amused voice from somewhere above us. “And here you are again. Ethan Chase, your family does have a knack for getting into trouble.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br><br>He is angry at fey for everything they did to him, but he is also paranoid and conserved. But then Kenzie made him open up slowly….and eventually, he fell in love (<i>Classic isn't it, for some reason YA heroines fall for YA bad boys... when will it stop?</i>). <br><br>He may have had irritated me for few moments, with constant pushing of everyone away and for being angry at Meghan for having no other choice (<i> she tried to protect them the best she could</i>), but I liked him anyway. I was angry at some points at him because of his quick judgment and condemning. But overall, he was interesting human.<br><br><b>His relationship with Kenzie was so fun to read about. </b> Kenzie balanced his grim moods and she always looked for a bright side when Ethan thought there was no other way. They are the perfect match for each other ♥.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “A pretty handsome jerk, I might add, but a huge, colossal megajerk nonetheless." Kenzie gave me a quick glance to see how I was taking this. I shrugged.<br>Not going to argue with that.<br>And then a second later:<br>She thought I was handsome?” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br> <i>
  <b>Serious spoilers:</b>
</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I kind of hated when he thought about Meghan like she was at fault for having to go away to protect her family. Also, I love how he hates Ash (good boy *pets*). Anyway, his relationship with Keirran was quite amusing, especially when he found out that he was his uncle…. Hahahhaha I laughed so much at that revelation. Anyway, I dread to think what will happen if that iron’s prophecy comes true.<br>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Kenzie </u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br><b>The off-limits girl, the one who is untouchable, rich and famous is a school reporter. </b>And she has the urge to know everything that is going on, including interviewing the new student Ethan (<i> of course... curiosity killed the cat</i>). Being persistent she haunts Ethan whenever she has the chance (<i>stalker much?</i>). But when she is drawn in the world of fey, she shows her that she is in fact brave, curious, impulsive, reckless, smart and very funny. She accepts the situation she was in because she wants to learn as much as she can about everything she can.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> “The Nevernever," she murmured, almost to herself, "I'm in the Nevernever. I'm in freaking faeryland.” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b><br>I love how awesome she was, brave and always being positive. After learning her secret I was devastated because it hurts me to know what will happen. </b><br><br><i>
  <b>Serious – really - spoilers:</b>
</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was so sad when I found out that she has <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[leukemia and that she would die soon. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But I can understand her making a choice for trading month of her life for Sight, because it made her see and feel something that she would never have. And she did it for Ethan too, so he wouldn’t be alone – to show him that it’s possible to have normal life with someone else.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Keirran &amp; Annwyl</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><b><br>Since they are the characters that don't appear until a certain point, i will put them in the spoilers :D </b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>I don't know what to think about Keirran...i just met him and he didn't leave big impression on me. He just seemed...ok. I liked him but that would be it.<br><br>He has no interest in Kenzie (<i>thank god! </i>) cause he is already in love with a exile summer faerie Annwyl. And he would do <i> anything </i> for her. Annwyl was ok character, not bad, but she needs more deepness in her character.<br><br>Anyway, he is the mysterious faery who appeared and offered the two of them(Kenzie and Ethan) to leave the Nevernever. Being shady and secretive, Ethan has no idea who he is. (<i> while those readers who have read Iron's Prophecy certainly know, because it's true and he is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ash's and Meghan's son  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br><br><i>
  <b>Serious – really - spoilers:</b>
</i><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I was disappointed when K didn't do anything while the guards almost chopped Ethan, he just sat there and waited...... idiot. Does he have a brain in that scene?????? Oh, Ash must spank his ass or something and then i will be satisfied <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>The old quartet: Meghan, Ash and Puck &amp; Grimalkin</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br><br>I was so happy to see them back ♥. Meghan has become such a kickass and great character ♥ Ash was still brooding and dark and gloomy as ever, but i kind of liked how "daddy" he was, lol. And Puck ♥♥♥ even though he wasn't that much present,i still swooned when he appeared ♥<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Care to join me, Goodfellow?”<br>“Oh, ice-boy. A moonlight stroll with you? Do you even have to ask?” </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>And lol Puck, LOL! <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br><blockquote><i><b> “Huh, another queen,” Puck mused, an evil grin crossing his face. “Maybe we should drop in and introduce ourselves, ice-boy. Do the whole, hey, we were just in the neighborhood, and we were just wondering if you had any plans to take over the Nevernever. Have a fruit basket.” </b></i></blockquote>
<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And Grimalkin.......you better start giving some answers instead of "i am a cat" answers...<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i>
    <u>Everyone else:</u>
  </i>
</b>:<br>◉ <b>Todd </b> was cute, interesting and i loved how he pestered Ethan, mwahahahahah! And i just liked him :D (<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ sad over what happened to him in the end of the book T_T, that he lost his memory and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ feyness  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>◉ <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b> Leanan</b> who is still crazy and scary and awesome as ever :D  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>◉ Did i miss anyone? O_o<br><br><blockquote> <b>► OVERALL</b>: </blockquote><br><br>HOLLY COW, THIS IS ONE OF THE BIGGEST REVIEWS I HAVE EVER WRITTEN o_O. <br>Other than that, i loved it, enjoyed it, was sucked in it, because Kagawa is awesome writer and she always puts enough details so you can imagine it always... And also, i cannot wait to see what sequel will have for me in store next, i just can't wait to read it. That is all. And if the worst thing happens, i'll just... go into a corner and cry.<br><br>I want the next book noooooooooooooooooooooooooow T____________________T<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376685i/731671.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_227253218" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/227253218" />
    <a title="Whitney" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3827678-whitney"><img alt="Whitney" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580343008p2/3827678.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/227253218?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney" href="/user/show/3827678-whitney">Whitney</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=2012-favorites">2012-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=blown-away">blown-away</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=just-loooooved-it">just-loooooved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=neat-plot">neat-plot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=okay-heroines">okay-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=right-in-the-feels">right-in-the-feels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=that-ending-omg">that-ending-omg</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=lick-this-cover">lick-this-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=surprised-as-hell">surprised-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3827678-whitney?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer227253218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4670720085329573890">You can see this review on my blog <a href='http://burnt-pages.blogspot.com/2012/08/early-review-lost-prince-by-julie-kagawa.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a>. c:<br/><br/>First off, spoilers ahead! If you haven't read The Iron Fey series, I suggest you just step away from the review. ._.<br/><br/><i>The Lost Prince</i> is about Meghan Chase's little brother--whom we all know him from TIF series as the one who got kidnapped and brought to the Nevernever in <i>The Iron King</i>--and he's changed. A. Lot. Then when his half-breed Phouka friend goes missing, and sightings of mysterious creepy Fey suddenly spring up, Ethan has to get involved in som</span>
  <span id="freeText4670720085329573890" style="display:none">You can see this review on my blog <a href="http://burnt-pages.blogspot.com/2012/08/early-review-lost-prince-by-julie-kagawa.html" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>. c:<br><br>First off, spoilers ahead! If you haven't read The Iron Fey series, I suggest you just step away from the review. ._.<br><br><i>The Lost Prince</i> is about Meghan Chase's little brother--whom we all know him from TIF series as the one who got kidnapped and brought to the Nevernever in <i>The Iron King</i>--and he's changed. A. Lot. Then when his half-breed Phouka friend goes missing, and sightings of mysterious creepy Fey suddenly spring up, Ethan has to get involved in something he's been avoiding ever since Meghan left him.<br><br>I have to say that this was a hella awesome read, but it had some disappointments in here and there. But to begin the actual review, the plot was super cool. The main problem in the Nevernever is everything dying off--if you've read TIF series, you'll already know this. And then there are faeries that spring up out of no where when Ethan's friend goes missing. They're the faeries that children forgot about, their Glamour ran on the children's imagination, if I'm not mistaken. (It's been a almost a whole bloody year since I've read about TIF. ;-;) That's all I'll say about that because I already feel like I'm spoiling everything. ;P But I thought the plot was awesomely neat and a clever point to be made since it's been stated in TIF. That means old characters show up. &lt;333<br><br>As for characters, Ethan to me, he's kind of a bastard. He's rude to everyone he encounters, though I understand why he does it. He doesn't want to get involved with anyone, and especially nobody with him. But there's not really much to say about him since he's nothing like Meghan--well he's stubborn, but other than that, nothing. To me at least. And what's up with the tattoos on the cover model's body? There's absolutely no mention of him having tattoos in the book. *drools confusingly though*<br><br>The love interest. I felt like my head was about to explode every time Kenzie opened her mouth. I seriously wanted to wrestle a rabid bear than walk through the Nevernever with her stubborn-ass like Ethan did. I could endure Ethan, but she was just getting on my nerves really bad lol. By the end of the book, I understand her a little better. Do I feel sorry for her? Yes. Do I like her because of it? No. Call me shallow or whatever, but when I start disliking a character as much as I did Kenzie in the beginning, it's hard for me to like them. Granted, I dislike her less now. xD But I was surprised when she came out about her "secret." I'm just wondering how that will effect her and Ethan's relationship.<br><br>And I'd like to say that there wasn't enough Puck in this. But I get it that this is in a whole new perspective and holy shit I'm missing them...BUT DAMMIT I LOVE PUCK. :'c And the cameos Ash and Meg made just made me fangirl all over the place. Like as soon as Ash was mentioned but not really...as soon as he was <i>described</i>, I was like, "Omfg, I just wet my pants a little. MY FEELS CANNOT CONTAIN THIS ABOUT OF EMOTIONS." But then it just all died down when Keirran came into the picture. He wasn't anything I expected him to be. Ash's son... He's...he's...no. I just can't. I AM DISAPPOINTED. I knew it was him when Ethan saw him outside of Meg's home. I. Knew. It. And you can tell Puck didn't want to be in Keirran's presence. I felt SO sorry for him I JUST WANTED TO SHRINK HIM DOWN AND PUT HIM IN MY CLEAVAGE FOREVER. I mean... ._. Cuddle him. Wait. Nevermind. But there was Grimalkin in here too. &lt;3 Who doesn't love Grim after reading these books?!<br><br>I'm glad the ending wasn't as bad as I thought it would be, because it's not really a cliffhanger. And the title of the next books is obvious going to circle around one character in particular. But it ended off in me disliking Keirran even more. <br><br>I'm so glad I got sucked back into this world; I was missing it terribly after I finished <i>The Iron Knight</i> almost one year ago. *nostalgic sigh* Julie creates such mind-bending books, it's so unreal. I loved it. &lt;3 Other than the minor flaws, I loved this book, but just couldn't give it five stars. And I'm mad at myself for doing such a horrific act for one of Julie Kagawa's books. I MEAN SHE JUST FOLLOWED ME ON TWITTER AND NOW I WROTE THIS REVIEW. I'M GONNA CRY MYSELF TO SLEEP FOR FOREVER IS SHE UNFOLLOWS MEEEEE. <br><br>But this cover.... Ethan has forever changed from a little boy to just a pile of steaming hotness.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380744146ra/3118288.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4670720085329573890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=cover-lust">cover-lust</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer304073917" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13735319284020543095"><i>ARC supplied by NetGalley and Harlequin Teen in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/><b>3.5</b><br/><br/>THE LOST PRINCE.<br/><br/>What can I say about this book? When I was approved for the ARC, I nearly passed out. I kid you not; I chucked my iTouch across the room where it hit the wall and fell on Kipper, who was luckily so focused on my excitement he completely ignored it.<br/><br/>I grabbed my Nook, plugged it into my laptop, and had a teenage angst attack for about fifteen minutes when I couldn't remember how to drag the file to my </span>
  <span id="freeText13735319284020543095" style="display:none"><i>ARC supplied by NetGalley and Harlequin Teen in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br><b>3.5</b><br><br>THE LOST PRINCE.<br><br>What can I say about this book? When I was approved for the ARC, I nearly passed out. I kid you not; I chucked my iTouch across the room where it hit the wall and fell on Kipper, who was luckily so focused on my excitement he completely ignored it.<br><br>I grabbed my Nook, plugged it into my laptop, and had a teenage angst attack for about fifteen minutes when I couldn't remember how to drag the file to my Nook folder. Really, Zuko would have been proud. <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/zuko%20angst/Kelila14/GIFs/Reaction%20GIFs/Zukough.gif?o=3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373805ra/727552.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After I finally figured out how to do it, I curled up on the couch and read half the book in one sitting, though by no means in one <i>position</i>.<br><br> I was so excited to see <a href="&lt;a%20href=" rel="nofollow noopener">Ash, Meghan, and Puck</a>, I rushed through the book until I reached them. Then I re-read it. After fangirling for quite a bit, I went to bed, and as soon as I awoke, continued my journey and finally finished the book. My face after I finally snapped shut the cover on my e-book?<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/disappointed%20gifs/shikhee/Gifs/ae04249f.gif?o=16" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373805ra/727553.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Disappointment.</i><br><br>I adore Julie Kagawa books, and I don't think I've ever given one lower than four stars. But THE LOST PRINCE was a little different, and i'm about to explain why.<br><br><b>Plot</b><br><br>"Call of the Forgotten", the series name, gives you more than you might realize. Half-bloods, dryads - mostly creatures of the fey have been disappearing. The cause? Misty, horrifying fey, much like those seen in the Forgotten village of THE IRON KNIGHT. They are the Forgotten - fey that no one remembers anymore. Sucking the glamour out of remembered fey like sick faery vampires makes them more real. Afraid for his life, Todd, a half-phouka, turns to Ethan for protection, only for him to also disappear. After that, trying to silence Ethan, The Forgotten attempt to kill Ethan and Kenzie, his ‘friend’ from school. Realizing (with help) he must inform The Iron Queen, he ventures into the Neverever and from there, Ethan, Kenzie, and a special ‘guest’ embark on a little journey.<br><br>It truly was a fantastic plot, strengthened by the mystery behind the ruler of the Forgotten, and the tiny amount of sympathy behind their reasoning.<br><br><b>Characters</b><br><br>Ethan Chase. Remember the adorable little boy with his curly brown hair and bright eyes and- ahhhh! *pinches cheeks* He's was so cuuuute!<br><br>This boy does not remain. He's a delinquent, your YA bad-boy. It's mostly <i>their</i> fault, as he refers to the Fey, however. He's also an absolute douche. Ethan, of course, has his reasons for being this way, but if you're the unforgiving type, you won't like Ethan in the first few chapters. Books from male's point of views are a little tricky to navigate through, and Julie did it flawlessly in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9659607.The_Iron_Knight__The_Iron_Fey___4_" title="The Iron Knight (The Iron Fey, #4) by Julie Kagawa" rel="nofollow noopener">THE IRON KNIGHT</a> with Ash, one of my forever loves. However, I couldn't connect to Ethan in this book. I didn't like him most of the time. I mean, sure, he's unbelievable sexy, but I felt like a cougar. I mean, this is Meghan's little brother. The last time I saw him he was four.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379773582i/319510.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kenzie St. James. This girl. I mean really. She's a brave little thing, but she's also nosy. The pretty, popular girl who works as an editor on the school newspaper. Kenzie lives in a home where her rich-ass father mostly ignores her after her mother's death. Kenzie gets dragged into this mess after - you guessed it - prying and being a stubborn little mule. After that, Julie decides to shock us - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ It's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11870085.The_Fault_in_Our_Stars" title="The Fault in Our Stars by John Green" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fault in Our Stars</a>: Paranormal Edition. Kind of. Kenize has cancer. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>...<br><br>Keirran. Yes, Ash's visions came true. I shrieked when he was first seen; I <i>knew</i> it was him, the son of Ash and Meghan. The beautiful silver-haired, blue-eyed not-quite-fey, the Prince of the thrown and the nephew of Ethan. But as I dove further through THE IRON PRINCE, I found myself disliking him, more and more. By the end I hated him. He is nothing like his father, or his mother. The things he did were stupid; his soft heart won over his head in important situations. Keirran's summer fey love, Anwyln, had no personality. She was equally naive as Keirran (except this time, it was 24/7), and her character was plain as a sheet. I have no idea what he saw in her.<br><br>The Original Trio. Their appearance saves this book nearly a whole half-star, even if was brief. Meghan, Puck, and Ash will always be first in my hearts, just like the original team Avatar will always be better (to me) than the second one. Yet...they've changed. Meghan isn't as light-hearted; Ash is solemn as well, even after he gained a soul. Fatherhood has changed them both - or perhaps it's because we don't have a scene with them alone. Puck seems like the only one who's still <i>himself</i>, and I was thrilled for that. I just hope he finds some amazing badass lover, though, and <i>soon</i>. <br><br>*drumroll, please* And, of course, you can’t forget ... Grimalkin!<br><br><b>Writing</b><br>Once again, Julie demonstrates her exquisite writing ability. It is fluent and lyrical, easy to read but not overly- flowery or formal, which I enjoy. Rambling, confusing writing is not good writing. There is barely any humor in THE LOST PRINCE, however. We are suffering from the absence of Puck.<br><br>Perhaps I will grow into this series as the rest of the book is released, but for now I am content re-reading the brilliant original series by the talented Julie Kagawa.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13735319284020543095" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
